  <script>
   $(window).load( function(){
  			$.ajax({
  				type: "POST",
  				url: "/info-wGlobal/wGlobal/scripts/inc.mobile-switch.php?ajax=1",
  				dataType: "html",
  				cache: false,
  				success: function(html) {
  					if(html=='mobile'){
              if( $('html').attr('lang') == 'de' ){
                lang = 'Zur mobilen Version wechseln?';
                domain = 'https://m.zu.de';
              }else{
                lang = 'Swtich to the mobile site?';
                domain = 'https://m.zeppelin-university.com/';
              }
              check = confirm(lang);
              if (check == true) {
                window.location = domain;
              }
  					}
  				}
  			});
      });
  </script>

     <h1>
      Wir feiern Fragen.
     </h1>
     <p class="hyphenate">
      Die Frage ist Ursprung und Ausgangspunkt von Wissenschaft. Unsere universitäre Website fokussiert daher immer auf eine Frage. Fragen rund um Forschung, Lehre, Weiterbildung, wissenschaftliche Dienstleistungen und aus dem ZU-Universitätsleben werden hier gestellt. Zudem ist die Startseite eine Bühne für Ihre ganz persönlichen Fragen. So wie der französische Philosoph Jacques Derrida im Jahr 1998 bei seinem Vortrag an der Stanford University zum Thema „Die unbedingte Universität“ erklärte: „Eine Universität müsste also auch ein Ort sein, an dem nichts außer Frage steht.“
     </p>
     <br/>
     <br/>
     <h2>
      Fragen Sie uns ruhig mal. Wir freuen uns!
     </h2>

   <script>
    var TYPE_VIDEO = 2;
var TYPE_IMAGE = 1;
var TYPE_AUDIO = 3;

var archiveMode = 0;
var currentId = 0;
var currentLogoColor = "";
var url = "";

$('.zu-slideshow').on('cycle-update-view', function(event, optionHash, slideOptionsHash, currentSlideEl){

    // Change logo color
    currentLogoColor = $(currentSlideEl).data('layout');

    var optionHash = optionHash;


    // Only change color, when navigation is hidden
    if($('#blockNavigationOuter').css('top') == '-138px'){
        $('div.blockLogo img').attr('src', url + '/info-wGlobal/wGlobal/layout/images/logo-claim-' + $(currentSlideEl).data('layout') + '.png');
    }else{
        $('div.blockLogo img').attr('src', url + '/info-wGlobal/wGlobal/layout/images/logo-claim-black.png');
    }

    var link = $(currentSlideEl).data('link');
    $('div.link-overlay a').attr('href', link);

    if($(currentSlideEl).data('type') == TYPE_VIDEO || $(currentSlideEl).data('type') == TYPE_AUDIO){
        $('div.link-overlay a').hide();
        $('.zu-slideshow').cycle('pause');
        currentId = $(currentSlideEl).data('id');
        var player = document.getElementById(currentId);
        $(player).bind('ended', function(){
            $(player).unbind('ended');
            endArchiveMode(optionHash);
            $('div.link-overlay').unbind('click');
            $('.zu-slideshow').cycle('next');
            $('.zu-slideshow').cycle('resume');
            $('div.link-overlay a').hide();
        });

        var timeOut = setTimeout(function(){
            // Set play button in overlay for tablets
            if($('html').hasClass('touch')){
                $('div.link-overlay').addClass('touch');
            }
            clearTimeout(timeOut);
        },100);


        $(player).bind('play', '#'+currentId, function(){
            var timeOut = setTimeout(function(){
                // Remove the play button in overlay for tablets
                $('div.link-overlay').removeClass('touch');
                clearTimeout(timeOut);
            },100);
            $(player).unbind('play');
            $('div.link-overlay a').show();
        });

        /**
         *  For tablets
         */
        $('div.link-overlay').bind('click', function(){
            if(player.currentTime > 0 ){
                window.location.href = link;
                return false;
            }
            player.play();
        });

        player.play();
    }

    if($(currentSlideEl).data('type') == TYPE_IMAGE){
        $('div.link-overlay a').show();
        setTimeout(function(){
            endArchiveMode(optionHash)
            $('div.link-overlay a').show();
        },parseInt($(currentSlideEl).data('cycle-timeout'))-500);
    }


    resize();

});


// events
$(window).on('resize', function(e) {
    resize();
    scale($(document).scrollTop());
})

$(window).on('scroll', function(){
    scale($(document).scrollTop());
});


$('#navigationControl').on('click', function(){
    showMenu();
    hideSlider();
    ga('send', 'event', 'Startseite', 'click', 'Navigation');
});

$('div.archive-button').on('click', function(){
    showArchive();
    ga('send', 'event', 'Startseite', 'click', 'Archiv');
});

$('div.slider-button').on('click', function(){
    hideMenu();
    showSlider();
    ga('send', 'event', 'Startseite', 'click', 'Frage');
});

$('div.side-container-wrapper div.close-button').on('click', function(){
    hideSlider();
    showMenu();
});

$('div.archive-wrapper div.close-button').on('click', function(){
    hideArchive();
    showMenu();
});

$('div.archive-more').on('click', function(){

    $('div.archive-wrapper div.row').children('.theme-box').each(function(index){
        $(this).removeClass('hidden');
    });

    $(this).hide();

    $(".archive-wrapper div.row").mCustomScrollbar({
        advanced:{
            updateOnContentResize: true
        }
    });

});

var endArchiveMode = function(optionHash){
    if(archiveMode == 1 && optionHash.currSlide == (optionHash.slideCount)-1){
        $('.zu-slideshow').cycle('stop');
        window.location.href = '/#showArchive';
        return false;
    }
}

/**
 * Form
 */

$('div.circle a').on('click', function(){

    var email, message;
    var e = $(this);

    email = $('input[name="startquestion[email]"]').val().replace($('input[name="startquestion[email]"]').data('rel'), '');
    message  = $('div.message').html().replace(/(<([^>]+)>)/ig,"").trim().replace($('div.message').data('default'), '');

    $.ajax({
        type: "POST",
        url: "/",
        data: {'startquestion[email]': email,'startquestion[question]': message},
        beforeSend: function()
        {
            e.parent('div').addClass('loading');
        },
        success: function(data)
        {
            e.parent('div').removeClass('loading');



            if(data.success == false){
                $.each(data.post.startquestion, function(index, value){


                    console.log(index);
                    console.log(value);

                    if(index == "question" && value == ""){
                        $('div[name="startquestion['+index+']"]').addClass("error");
                    }
                    if(index == "email" && validateEmail(value) === false){
                        $('input[name="startquestion['+index+']"]').addClass("error");
                    }
                });

                $('div.errorMessage').fadeIn();
            }else{
                $('div.errorMessage').hide();
                $('#form-question').hide();
                $('div.form-finished').fadeIn();
            }
        }
    });

});

var hideArchive = function(){
    $('div.archive-container').animate({'bottom': '-521px'}, {
            duration: 'slow',
            start: function(){
                $('body').css('overflow', 'hidden');
            },
            done: function(){
                $('body').css('overflow', 'auto');
                $('div.archive-container').hide();
            }
        },
        function(){
            $('#side-container').hide();
        });
};

var showSlider = function(){
    $('#side-container').show();
    $('#side-container').animate({'left': '0px'}, {
        duration: 'slow',
        start: function(){
            if($('#blockNavigationOuter').css('top') == '0px'){
                //$('#navigationControl').trigger('click');
                //$('#navigationControl').show();
            }
        }
    }, function(){

    });

    if($('div.archive-container').css('bottom') == "0px"){
        hideArchive();
    }
};

var hideSlider = function(){
    $('#side-container').animate({'left': '-680px'}, 'slow', function(){
        $('#side-container').hide();
    });
};

var resize = function() {
    var width = $(window).width(),
        pWidth, // player width, to be defined
        height = $(window).height(),
        pHeight, // player height, tbd
        container = $('#' + currentId);

    // when screen aspect ratio differs from video, video must center and underlay one dimension
    if (width / (16/9) < height) { // if new video height < window height (gap underneath)
        pWidth = Math.ceil(height * (16/9)); // get new player width
        container.width(pWidth).height(height).css({left: (width - pWidth) / 2, top: 0}); // player width is greater, offset left; reset top
    } else { // new video width < window width (gap to right)
        pHeight = Math.ceil(width / (16/9)); // get new player height
        container.width(width).height(pHeight).css({left: 0, top: (height - pHeight) / 2}); // player height is greater, offset top; reset left
    }
};


var scale = function(addme){

    console.log(addme);
    var h = $(window).height();
    $('#side-container').height(h+addme);
    $('.side-container-wrapper').height(h+addme);
};

var validateEmail = function(email) {
    var re = /^(([^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+(\.[^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+)*)|(\".+\"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
    return re.test(email);
};

var showMenu = function(){
    if($('#blockNavigationOuter').css('top') == '-138px'){
        if($('#side-container').is(':visible')){
            //hideSlider();
        }
        $('#blockNavigationOuter').animate({'top': '0px'}, {
            duration: 'slow',
            start: function(){
                $('div.blockLogo img').attr('src', url + '/info-wGlobal/wGlobal/layout/images/logo-claim-black.png');
                $('#navigationControl').hide();
            }
        }, function(){

        });
    }else{
        $('#blockNavigationOuter').animate({'top': '-138px'}, 'slow', function(){
            $('div.blockLogo img').attr('src', url + '/info-wGlobal/wGlobal/layout/images/logo-claim-'+currentLogoColor+'.png');
        });
    }

    if($('#blockBottom').css('bottom') == '-32px'){
        $('#blockBottom').animate({'bottom': '0px'}, {duration: 'slow'}, function(){});
        $('.archive-button').animate({'bottom': '31px'}, {duration: 'slow'}, function(){});

    }else{
        $('#blockBottom').animate({'bottom': '-32px'}, 'slow', function(){});
        $('.archive-button').animate({'bottom': '31px'}, {duration: 'slow'}, function(){});
    }

    if($('div.archive-container').css('bottom') == "0px"){
        hideArchive();
    }
};

var hideMenu = function(){
    $('#blockNavigationOuter').animate({'top': '-138px'}, 'slow', function(){
        $('div.blockLogo img').attr('src', url +'/info-wGlobal/wGlobal/layout/images/logo-claim-'+currentLogoColor+'.png');
        $('#navigationControl').show();
    });
    $('#blockBottom').animate({'bottom': '-32px'}, 'slow', function(){});
    $('.archive-button').animate({'bottom': '0px'}, {duration: 'slow'}, function(){});
};

var showArchive = function(){
    hideMenu();
    $('div.archive-container').animate({'bottom': '0px'}, {
        duration: 'slow',
        start: function(){
            $('div.archive-container').show();
            $('body').css('overflow', 'hidden');
        },
        done: function(){
            $('body').css('overflow', 'auto');
        }
    }, function(){

    });

    if($('#side-container').css('left') == "0px"){
        hideSlider();
    }

    if($('#blockNavigationOuter').css('left') == "0px"){
        hideMenu();
    }
};

(function(){

    $('.zu-slideshow').cycle();
    resize();
    scale($(document).scrollTop());


    if(window.location.hash == "#showArchive"){
        $('div.archive-button').trigger('click');
    };

    $('div.link-overlay a').bind('click', function(){
        ga('send', 'event', 'Startseite', 'click', $(this).attr('href'));
    });

    $('div.blockLogo img').bind('click', function(){
        ga('send', 'event', 'Startseite', 'click', 'Logo');
    });

})();
   </script>
  </div>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(function(){
                    var timer;

                    $(window).load(function(){
                        setTimeout(function () {
                            setApplicationBox("open");

                            timer = setTimeout(function () {
                                setApplicationBox("close");
                            }, 5000);

                        }, 500);
                    });

                    $("#blockApplication").hover(
                        function(){
                            clearTimeout(timer);
                        }, function(){
                            timer = setTimeout(function () {
                                setApplicationBox("close");
                            }, 5000);
                        }
                    );

                    $("#btnApplication").click(function () {
                        setApplicationBox("open");
                    });

                    $("#blockApplication .close").click(function () {
                        setApplicationBox("close");
                    });

                    $("#navigationControl").click(function () {
                        $('#btnApplication').animate({'bottom': '28px'}, {
                            duration: 'slow'
                        }, function(){});
                        $('#blockApplication').animate({'bottom': '28px'}, {
                            duration: 'slow'
                        }, function(){});
                    });

                    function setApplicationBox(mode) {
                        if(mode === 'close'){
                            $("#blockApplication").removeClass("open");

                            setTimeout(function () {
                                $("#btnApplication").removeClass("hide");
                            }, 400);
                        } else {
                            $("#btnApplication").addClass("hide");

                            setTimeout(function () {
                                $("#blockApplication").addClass("open");
                            }, 400);
                        }
                    }

                    $('#blockApplication a.button').on('click', function(){
                        ga('send', 'event', 'Startseite', 'click', 'Jetzt Anmelden');
                    });
                });
  </script>

        <script>
         //<![CDATA[
		function calcCenter() {
			$(".centerfix").each(function() {
				width = $(this).width();
				//console.log("width"+width);
				if(width > 0) {
					parentWidth = $(this).parent().width();
					//console.log("parentWidth"+parentWidth);
					margin = (parentWidth-width)/2;
					//console.log("margin"+margin);
					$(this).css( { marginLeft : margin} );
				}
			});
		}
		
		jQuery(document).ready(function(){ 
		
			calcCenter();
		
			// Erstes Dropdown
			$("ul#serviceFooterLevel1").on("click", ".init", function() {
				$(this).closest("ul#serviceFooterLevel1").children("li:not(.init)").toggle();
				allOptions2.hide();
			});
			var value1_old;
			var allOptions = $("ul#serviceFooterLevel1").children("li:not(.init)");
			$("ul#serviceFooterLevel1").on("click", "li:not(.init)", function() {
				//console.log("click1");
				allOptions.removeClass("selected");
				$(this).addClass("selected");
				var value1 = $("ul#serviceFooterLevel1").find(".selected").data("value");
				//console.log(value1);
				//console.log(value1_old);				
				if(value1 != value1_old) {
					//console.log("neu");
					value1_old = value1;
					$("ul#serviceFooterLevel1").children(".init").html($(this).html());
					$(".serviceFooterLevel2 ul").children(".init").html("bitte wählen");

					$(".serviceFooterLevel2").hide();
					$(".serviceFooterLevel2").removeClass("active");
					$("#serviceFooterSubmit").removeClass("active");
					allOptions2.removeClass("selected");
				}
				allOptions.toggle();
				
				$("#serviceFooterLevel2_"+value1).fadeIn("slow");
				
				$("#serviceFooterLevel2_"+value1).addClass("active");
				
				allOptions2.hide();
				calcCenter();	
			});
			
			
			
			$(".serviceFooterLevel2 ul").on("click", ".init", function() {
				
				var count = $(".serviceFooterLevel2.active ul li").length;
				
				if(count > 6) {
					$(".serviceFooterLevel2.active ul li").addClass("openTop");
				}
				$(this).closest(".serviceFooterLevel2 ul").children("li:not(.init)").toggle();
				
				allOptions.hide();
				
			});

			var allOptions2 = $(".serviceFooterLevel2 ul").children("li:not(.init)");
			$(".serviceFooterLevel2 ul").on("click", "li:not(.init)", function() {
				//console.log("click2");
				
				allOptions2.removeClass("selected");
				$(this).addClass("selected");
				$(this).parent().children(".init").html($(this).html());
				allOptions2.toggle();
				var value2 = $(".serviceFooterLevel2 ul").find(".selected").data("value");
				//console.log(value2);	
				if(value2) $("#serviceFooterSubmit").addClass("active");
				calcCenter();
				
				
			});
			
			$("#serviceFooterSubmit").click(function(event){ 
				event.preventDefault();
				var value2 = $(".serviceFooterLevel2 ul").find(".selected").data("value");
				//console.log(value2);
				if(value2) window.location.href = value2;
			});
			
		});
		//]]>
        </script>

    $(window).load( function(){
   			$.ajax({
   				type: "POST",
   				url: "/info-wGlobal/wGlobal/scripts/inc.mobile-switch.php?ajax=1",
   				dataType: "html",
   				cache: false,
   				success: function(html) {
   					if(html=='mobile'){
               if( $('html').attr('lang') == 'de' ){
                 lang = 'Zur mobilen Version wechseln?';
                 domain = 'https://m.zu.de';
               }else{
                 lang = 'Swtich to the mobile site?';
                 domain = 'https://m.zeppelin-university.com/';
               }
               check = confirm(lang);
               if (check == true) {
                 window.location = domain;
               }
   					}
   				}
   			});
       });
   </script>

      <h1>
       Wir feiern Fragen.
      </h1>
      <p class="hyphenate">
       Die Frage ist Ursprung und Ausgangspunkt von Wissenschaft. Unsere universitäre Website fokussiert daher immer auf eine Frage. Fragen rund um Forschung, Lehre, Weiterbildung, wissenschaftliche Dienstleistungen und aus dem ZU-Universitätsleben werden hier gestellt. Zudem ist die Startseite eine Bühne für Ihre ganz persönlichen Fragen. So wie der französische Philosoph Jacques Derrida im Jahr 1998 bei seinem Vortrag an der Stanford University zum Thema „Die unbedingte Universität“ erklärte: „Eine Universität müsste also auch ein Ort sein, an dem nichts außer Frage steht.“
      </p>
      <br/>
      <br/>
      <h2>
       Fragen Sie uns ruhig mal. Wir freuen uns!
      </h2>
      <br/>
      <br/>
      <div id="form-question">
       <div class="form-group">
        <input class="inputEmailFrom" data-rel="E-Mail-Adresse:" name="startquestion[email]" type="text" value="E-Mail-Adresse:"/>
       </div>
       <br/>
       <div class="outer">
        <div class="inner message" contenteditable="true" data-default="Ihre Frage:" name="startquestion[question]">
         Ihre Frage:
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="circle">
        <a href="#">
         Senden
        </a>
       </div>
       <div class="errorMessage">
        Bitte überprüfen Sie ihre Angaben.
       </div>
       <br/>
       <br/>
      </div>
      <div class="form-finished">
       Vielen Dank für Ihre Frage.
       <br/>
       Wir geben Ihnen so bald wie möglich eine Antwort.
      </div>
     </div>

    <script>
     var TYPE_VIDEO = 2;
 var TYPE_IMAGE = 1;
 var TYPE_AUDIO = 3;
 
 var archiveMode = 0;
 var currentId = 0;
 var currentLogoColor = "";
 var url = "";
 
 $('.zu-slideshow').on('cycle-update-view', function(event, optionHash, slideOptionsHash, currentSlideEl){
 
     // Change logo color
     currentLogoColor = $(currentSlideEl).data('layout');
 
     var optionHash = optionHash;
 
 
     // Only change color, when navigation is hidden
     if($('#blockNavigationOuter').css('top') == '-138px'){
         $('div.blockLogo img').attr('src', url + '/info-wGlobal/wGlobal/layout/images/logo-claim-' + $(currentSlideEl).data('layout') + '.png');
     }else{
         $('div.blockLogo img').attr('src', url + '/info-wGlobal/wGlobal/layout/images/logo-claim-black.png');
     }
 
     var link = $(currentSlideEl).data('link');
     $('div.link-overlay a').attr('href', link);
 
     if($(currentSlideEl).data('type') == TYPE_VIDEO || $(currentSlideEl).data('type') == TYPE_AUDIO){
         $('div.link-overlay a').hide();
         $('.zu-slideshow').cycle('pause');
         currentId = $(currentSlideEl).data('id');
         var player = document.getElementById(currentId);
         $(player).bind('ended', function(){
             $(player).unbind('ended');
             endArchiveMode(optionHash);
             $('div.link-overlay').unbind('click');
             $('.zu-slideshow').cycle('next');
             $('.zu-slideshow').cycle('resume');
             $('div.link-overlay a').hide();
         });
 
         var timeOut = setTimeout(function(){
             // Set play button in overlay for tablets
             if($('html').hasClass('touch')){
                 $('div.link-overlay').addClass('touch');
             }
             clearTimeout(timeOut);
         },100);
 
 
         $(player).bind('play', '#'+currentId, function(){
             var timeOut = setTimeout(function(){
                 // Remove the play button in overlay for tablets
                 $('div.link-overlay').removeClass('touch');
                 clearTimeout(timeOut);
             },100);
             $(player).unbind('play');
             $('div.link-overlay a').show();
         });
 
         /**
          *  For tablets
          */
         $('div.link-overlay').bind('click', function(){
             if(player.currentTime > 0 ){
                 window.location.href = link;
                 return false;
             }
             player.play();
         });
 
         player.play();
     }
 
     if($(currentSlideEl).data('type') == TYPE_IMAGE){
         $('div.link-overlay a').show();
         setTimeout(function(){
             endArchiveMode(optionHash)
             $('div.link-overlay a').show();
         },parseInt($(currentSlideEl).data('cycle-timeout'))-500);
     }
 
 
     resize();
 
 });
 
 
 // events

     resize();
     scale($(document).scrollTop());
 })
 
 $(window).on('scroll', function(){
     scale($(document).scrollTop());
 });

 });

 });

 });

 });
 
 $('div.archive-more').on('click', function(){
 
     $('div.archive-wrapper div.row').children('.theme-box').each(function(index){
         $(this).removeClass('hidden');
     });
 
     $(this).hide();
 
     $(".archive-wrapper div.row").mCustomScrollbar({
         advanced:{
             updateOnContentResize: true
         }
     });
 
 });
 
 var endArchiveMode = function(optionHash){
     if(archiveMode == 1 && optionHash.currSlide == (optionHash.slideCount)-1){
         $('.zu-slideshow').cycle('stop');
         window.location.href = '/#showArchive';
         return false;
     }
 }
 
 /**
  * Form
  */
 
 $('div.circle a').on('click', function(){
 
     var email, message;
     var e = $(this);
 
     email = $('input[name="startquestion[email]"]').val().replace($('input[name="startquestion[email]"]').data('rel'), '');
     message  = $('div.message').html().replace(/(<([^>]+)>)/ig,"").trim().replace($('div.message').data('default'), '');
 
     $.ajax({
         type: "POST",
         url: "/",
         data: {'startquestion[email]': email,'startquestion[question]': message},
         beforeSend: function()
         {
             e.parent('div').addClass('loading');
         },
         success: function(data)
         {
             e.parent('div').removeClass('loading');
 
 
 
             if(data.success == false){
                 $.each(data.post.startquestion, function(index, value){
 
 
                     console.log(index);
                     console.log(value);
 
                     if(index == "question" && value == ""){
                         $('div[name="startquestion['+index+']"]').addClass("error");
                     }
                     if(index == "email" && validateEmail(value) === false){
                         $('input[name="startquestion['+index+']"]').addClass("error");
                     }
                 });
 
                 $('div.errorMessage').fadeIn();
             }else{
                 $('div.errorMessage').hide();
                 $('#form-question').hide();
                 $('div.form-finished').fadeIn();
             }
         }
     });
 
 });
 
 var hideArchive = function(){
     $('div.archive-container').animate({'bottom': '-521px'}, {
             duration: 'slow',
             start: function(){
                 $('body').css('overflow', 'hidden');
             },
             done: function(){
                 $('body').css('overflow', 'auto');
                 $('div.archive-container').hide();
             }
         },
         function(){
             $('#side-container').hide();
         });
 };
 
 var showSlider = function(){
     $('#side-container').show();
     $('#side-container').animate({'left': '0px'}, {
         duration: 'slow',
         start: function(){
             if($('#blockNavigationOuter').css('top') == '0px'){
                 //$('#navigationControl').trigger('click');
                 //$('#navigationControl').show();
             }
         }
     }, function(){
 
     });
 
     if($('div.archive-container').css('bottom') == "0px"){
         hideArchive();
     }
 };
 
 var hideSlider = function(){
     $('#side-container').animate({'left': '-680px'}, 'slow', function(){
         $('#side-container').hide();
     });
 };
 
 var resize = function() {
     var width = $(window).width(),
         pWidth, // player width, to be defined
         height = $(window).height(),
         pHeight, // player height, tbd
         container = $('#' + currentId);
 
     // when screen aspect ratio differs from video, video must center and underlay one dimension
     if (width / (16/9) < height) { // if new video height < window height (gap underneath)
         pWidth = Math.ceil(height * (16/9)); // get new player width
         container.width(pWidth).height(height).css({left: (width - pWidth) / 2, top: 0}); // player width is greater, offset left; reset top
     } else { // new video width < window width (gap to right)
         pHeight = Math.ceil(width / (16/9)); // get new player height
         container.width(width).height(pHeight).css({left: 0, top: (height - pHeight) / 2}); // player height is greater, offset top; reset left
     }
 };
 
 
 var scale = function(addme){
 
     console.log(addme);
     var h = $(window).height();
     $('#side-container').height(h+addme);
     $('.side-container-wrapper').height(h+addme);
 };
 
 var validateEmail = function(email) {
     var re = /^(([^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+(\.[^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+)*)|(\".+\"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
     return re.test(email);
 };
 
 var showMenu = function(){
     if($('#blockNavigationOuter').css('top') == '-138px'){
         if($('#side-container').is(':visible')){
             //hideSlider();
         }
         $('#blockNavigationOuter').animate({'top': '0px'}, {
             duration: 'slow',
             start: function(){
                 $('div.blockLogo img').attr('src', url + '/info-wGlobal/wGlobal/layout/images/logo-claim-black.png');
                 $('#navigationControl').hide();
             }
         }, function(){
 
         });
     }else{
         $('#blockNavigationOuter').animate({'top': '-138px'}, 'slow', function(){
             $('div.blockLogo img').attr('src', url + '/info-wGlobal/wGlobal/layout/images/logo-claim-'+currentLogoColor+'.png');
         });
     }
 
     if($('#blockBottom').css('bottom') == '-32px'){
         $('#blockBottom').animate({'bottom': '0px'}, {duration: 'slow'}, function(){});
         $('.archive-button').animate({'bottom': '31px'}, {duration: 'slow'}, function(){});
 
     }else{
         $('#blockBottom').animate({'bottom': '-32px'}, 'slow', function(){});
         $('.archive-button').animate({'bottom': '31px'}, {duration: 'slow'}, function(){});
     }
 
     if($('div.archive-container').css('bottom') == "0px"){
         hideArchive();
     }
 };
 
 var hideMenu = function(){
     $('#blockNavigationOuter').animate({'top': '-138px'}, 'slow', function(){
         $('div.blockLogo img').attr('src', url +'/info-wGlobal/wGlobal/layout/images/logo-claim-'+currentLogoColor+'.png');
         $('#navigationControl').show();
     });
     $('#blockBottom').animate({'bottom': '-32px'}, 'slow', function(){});
     $('.archive-button').animate({'bottom': '0px'}, {duration: 'slow'}, function(){});
 };
 
 var showArchive = function(){
     hideMenu();
     $('div.archive-container').animate({'bottom': '0px'}, {
         duration: 'slow',
         start: function(){
             $('div.archive-container').show();
             $('body').css('overflow', 'hidden');
         },
         done: function(){
             $('body').css('overflow', 'auto');
         }
     }, function(){
 
     });
 
     if($('#side-container').css('left') == "0px"){
         hideSlider();
     }
 
     if($('#blockNavigationOuter').css('left') == "0px"){
         hideMenu();
     }
 };

     $('.zu-slideshow').cycle();
     resize();
     scale($(document).scrollTop());
 
 
     if(window.location.hash == "#showArchive"){
         $('div.archive-button').trigger('click');
     };
 
     $('div.link-overlay a').bind('click', function(){
         ga('send', 'event', 'Startseite', 'click', $(this).attr('href'));
     });
 
     $('div.blockLogo img').bind('click', function(){
         ga('send', 'event', 'Startseite', 'click', 'Logo');
     });
 
 })();
    </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(function(){
                     var timer;
 
                     $(window).load(function(){
                         setTimeout(function () {
                             setApplicationBox("open");
 
                             timer = setTimeout(function () {
                                 setApplicationBox("close");
                             }, 5000);
 
                         }, 500);
                     });
 
                     $("#blockApplication").hover(
                         function(){
                             clearTimeout(timer);
                         }, function(){
                             timer = setTimeout(function () {
                                 setApplicationBox("close");
                             }, 5000);
                         }
                     );
 
                     $("#btnApplication").click(function () {
                         setApplicationBox("open");
                     });
 
                     $("#blockApplication .close").click(function () {
                         setApplicationBox("close");
                     });
 
                     $("#navigationControl").click(function () {
                         $('#btnApplication').animate({'bottom': '28px'}, {
                             duration: 'slow'
                         }, function(){});
                         $('#blockApplication').animate({'bottom': '28px'}, {
                             duration: 'slow'
                         }, function(){});
                     });
 
                     function setApplicationBox(mode) {
                         if(mode === 'close'){
                             $("#blockApplication").removeClass("open");
 
                             setTimeout(function () {
                                 $("#btnApplication").removeClass("hide");
                             }, 400);
                         } else {
                             $("#btnApplication").addClass("hide");
 
                             setTimeout(function () {
                                 $("#blockApplication").addClass("open");
                             }, 400);
                         }
                     }
 
                     $('#blockApplication a.button').on('click', function(){
                         ga('send', 'event', 'Startseite', 'click', 'Jetzt Anmelden');
                     });
                 });
   </script>

         <script>
          //<![CDATA[
 		function calcCenter() {
 			$(".centerfix").each(function() {
 				width = $(this).width();
 				//console.log("width"+width);
 				if(width > 0) {
 					parentWidth = $(this).parent().width();
 					//console.log("parentWidth"+parentWidth);
 					margin = (parentWidth-width)/2;
 					//console.log("margin"+margin);
 					$(this).css( { marginLeft : margin} );
 				}
 			});
 		}
 		
 		jQuery(document).ready(function(){ 
 		
 			calcCenter();
 		
 			// Erstes Dropdown
 			$("ul#serviceFooterLevel1").on("click", ".init", function() {
 				$(this).closest("ul#serviceFooterLevel1").children("li:not(.init)").toggle();
 				allOptions2.hide();
 			});
 			var value1_old;
 			var allOptions = $("ul#serviceFooterLevel1").children("li:not(.init)");
 			$("ul#serviceFooterLevel1").on("click", "li:not(.init)", function() {
 				//console.log("click1");
 				allOptions.removeClass("selected");
 				$(this).addClass("selected");
 				var value1 = $("ul#serviceFooterLevel1").find(".selected").data("value");
 				//console.log(value1);
 				//console.log(value1_old);				
 				if(value1 != value1_old) {
 					//console.log("neu");
 					value1_old = value1;
 					$("ul#serviceFooterLevel1").children(".init").html($(this).html());
 					$(".serviceFooterLevel2 ul").children(".init").html("bitte wählen");
 
 					$(".serviceFooterLevel2").hide();
 					$(".serviceFooterLevel2").removeClass("active");
 					$("#serviceFooterSubmit").removeClass("active");
 					allOptions2.removeClass("selected");
 				}
 				allOptions.toggle();
 				
 				$("#serviceFooterLevel2_"+value1).fadeIn("slow");
 				
 				$("#serviceFooterLevel2_"+value1).addClass("active");
 				
 				allOptions2.hide();
 				calcCenter();	
 			});
 			
 			
 			
 			$(".serviceFooterLevel2 ul").on("click", ".init", function() {
 				
 				var count = $(".serviceFooterLevel2.active ul li").length;
 				
 				if(count > 6) {
 					$(".serviceFooterLevel2.active ul li").addClass("openTop");
 				}
 				$(this).closest(".serviceFooterLevel2 ul").children("li:not(.init)").toggle();
 				
 				allOptions.hide();
 				
 			});
 
 			var allOptions2 = $(".serviceFooterLevel2 ul").children("li:not(.init)");
 			$(".serviceFooterLevel2 ul").on("click", "li:not(.init)", function() {
 				//console.log("click2");
 				
 				allOptions2.removeClass("selected");
 				$(this).addClass("selected");
 				$(this).parent().children(".init").html($(this).html());
 				allOptions2.toggle();
 				var value2 = $(".serviceFooterLevel2 ul").find(".selected").data("value");
 				//console.log(value2);	
 				if(value2) $("#serviceFooterSubmit").addClass("active");
 				calcCenter();
 				
 				
 			});
 			
 			$("#serviceFooterSubmit").click(function(event){ 
 				event.preventDefault();
 				var value2 = $(".serviceFooterLevel2 ul").find(".selected").data("value");
 				//console.log(value2);
 				if(value2) window.location.href = value2;
 			});
 			
 		});
 		//]]>
         </script>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
